On the Qutb:
On the Qutb 
Sidi Ali Harazim (ra) said in Jawahir al-Maani:

وسألته رضي الله عن حقيقة القطبانية، فأجاب) رضي الله عنه بقوله : إعلم أن حقيقة القطبانية هي الخلافة
"And I asked him, may Allah be pleased with him, about the reality of Qutbaniyyah, to which he answered, may Allah be pleased with him, by saying: Know that the reality of Qutbaniyyah is the supreme caliphate
العظمى عن الحق مطلقاً في جميع الوجود جملة وتفصيلاً، حينما كان الرب إلهاً، كان هو خليفة في تصريف
representing the Absolute Truth in all of existence, both broadly and in detail. Wherever the Lord is God, he is the Caliph in administering
الحكم وتنفيذه في كل ما عليه ألوهية الله تعالى ثم قيامه بالبرزخية العظمى بين الحق والخلق، فلا يصل إلى الخلق
and implementing the divine decree over all that holds the divinity of Allah the Exalted, and then his standing in the supreme barrier between the Truth and creation, such that nothing of existence 
شيء كائناً ما كان من الحق، إلا بحكم القطب وتوليه ، ونيابته عن الحق في ذلك، وتوصيله كل قيمة إلى محلها، ثم
whatever it may be, reaches creation except by the decree of the Qutb and his management, and his representation of the Truth in that matter, and his conveying of every value to its place. Then,
قيامه في الوجود بروحانيته في كل ذرة من ذرات الوجود جملة وتفصيلاً، فترى الكون كله أشباحاً لا حركة لها، وإنما
his existence in spirituality in every atom of existence, both broadly and in detail, thus you see the entire universe as mere shadows without motion, but
هو الروح القائم فيها جملةً وتفصيلاً وقيامه فيها في أرواحها وأشباحها، ثم تصرفه في مراتب الأولياء، فيذوق
he is the spirit that stands in them in detail, existing in their spirits and shadows, then his management in the ranks of the saints, tasting
مختلفات أذواقهم، فلا تكون مرتبة في الوجود للعارفين والأولياء خارجة عن ذوقه فهو المتصرف في جميعها
their various experiences, so no rank in the existence of the knowers and the saints is outside his taste, for he manages all of them
والممد لأربابها وله الاختصاص بالسّر المكتوم، الذي لا مطمع لأحد في دركه والسلام.
and extends [support] to their masters, and he alone has the specialization in the secret concealed, which no one aspires to attain. Peace.

-Sidi Ali Harazim quoting Shaikh Ahmad al-Tijani, Jawaahir al Maani, vol. 2 (Dar al-Rashad, 197).

---
Age of the Soul:
Age of the Soul 
“The soul in its length is nine hundred thousand years long and so is its width," he said this about the soul of the Knowers, and as for others, they are like the pigeon or less.
 "And as for the dwelling of the soul of the general believers, the companions of the veil, it is from the first heaven to the fourth," and as for the fourth and above, the dwelling of the spirits of the Knowers varies according to their level. End quote from his dictation to us, may Allah be pleased with him."

And I heard him, may Allah be pleased with him, saying: Al-Shadhili, may Allah be pleased with him, said in his addressing the Truth, Glorious is His Majesty: Indeed, the disbeliever, even though he did not answer the call of Your faith, he has answered the call of Your sovereignty, so all comply with Your command, there is no creature but that You have a hold of its forelock, indeed my Lord is on a straight path. 

So, all that is in the universe, its animate and inanimate beings, indeed, the inanimate objects He, Glorified and Exalted be He, has endowed with souls that are not perceived and those souls are complete in the knowledge of Allah and with that knowledge, they glorify Allah, sanctify Him, prostrate to Him, and worship Him in the hearts, and as for the one who shows friendship outwardly but conceals enmity, then forsaking him is necessary. 

And as for cutting off his friendship and harmony by showing hostility and making complaints, this is not permissible, neither by religious law nor by natural disposition. and it is not attainable for someone with full intellect. to direct oneself to that, because Allah, Glorious and Exalted, has made this creation subject to the emergence of evil from them towards everyone, even if they are people of goodness."Because Allah manifests His glory at all times by a known command. and no time is free from His manifestation of evil through some of His creation. Thus, to confront and respond to that with evil entails great harm for the wise person, for every wise person must submit to the command of Allah in what He wills for His creation, and be humble before the command of Allah, showing gentleness and indifference, and by doing so, one escapes from the afflictions of its evil. 
And as for the one who confronts it with what appears to him to be the rightful response to evil, it will only increase for him in severity and burden, as a punishment for not recognizing the servitude which is characterized by humility and submission. Indeed, responding to evil is a departure from the bounds of servitude, and its doer is like one who adds fuel to the fire, which only increases in flames, and as for the one who resists it with humility, submission, and gentleness, the fire will soon be extinguished.
It is necessary for the servant who knows the intensity of enmity from someone to turn away from him or to show softness or indifference only to escape from his evil and to be cautious, of his creation, for creation is subject by the ordainment of Allah the Exalted, so nothing benefits with them except to turn away from what they are in of evil.
Al-Shafi'i, may Allah be pleased with him said: 
When I pardoned and did not harbor hatred against anyone, I relieved myself from the burden of grievances.
I greet my enemy upon seeing him, so as to remove evil from myself with greetings. And I am not saved from a friend who befriends me, so how can I be safe from the people of enmities? 
He says: 'The head of intellect, after faith, is to be amiable towards people.' 
We say: 'So it is obligatory first to extinguish their malice with kindness towards them, and if not, then by showing softness and humility to them, and if not, then by turning away from confronting them with evil.

Translators note: 
If one confronts evil with evil, this amplifies the severity and burden, comparable to adding fuel to a fire. If one adds fuel to the fire of evil, it diverges from the principle of servitude, which is diminished by humility and submission. If one diverges from the principle of servitude, they fail to align with wisdom, which requires submission to the divine command and humility before it. If one fails to align with wisdom, they cannot escape the afflictions of evil, as wisdom entails turning away from evil with softness or indifference. If one cannot escape the afflictions of evil, it is because they have not applied the necessary softness.”
 —Dr. A.L. Finch 

Bibliography:
Shaikh Ahmad al-Tijani. n.d. Jawaahir al-Ma’ani. Vol. 2, 226-227. Daar al Baydhaa: Daar al-Rashaad al-Hadathiyya.

The Harm of Creation:
The Harm of Creation 

*Precious advice from our Master, ash-Sheikh Ahmad Tijani, may Allah sanctify his secret:*

"... For the common people, due to their being veiled from Allah (Blessed and Exalted is He) and the majority of His decree, do not see, in their being inflicted with evil, anything other than the form of the person that inflicts it upon them. 

Thus, they rush to reciprocate evil with their own ability, deception, attacking with their own power. 
Thus, the intense evil rises over them. So, they are caged in the 
prison of punishment at every instant. 

Thus, when the evil of mankind is set upon the intelligent person, or they move to inflict it upon him, he sees that as a Divine self-disclosure, which no one can withstand, except through Divine support. 

Thus, the matter towards which his knowledge and intellect direct him is to return to Allah, fleeing and taking recourse in Him, 
constantly humbling himself and supplicating to Him and recognizing his incapacity and weakness. In other words, one should rush to seek refuge in Allah in defending them from His creation. 

There is no doubt that He will ward off all evil from them without any effort from themself. And if the flames of people’s evil should be ignited against them, they will be unable to reach them because they are protected by Allah (Exalted is He). Should someone be connected to Allah, nothing will be impossible for them. He (Blessed and Exalted is He) said: 
﴾Whomever fears Allah, He will grant them a way out. And He will provide for them from where they did not expect it. Whoever depends upon Allah, He suffices him﴿(al-Talaq, 2-3)"

- From the jewels of my master Ahmad at-Tijani, may Allah be pleased with him.
---
Construction of Zawiya in Fes:
Construction of Zawiya in Fes 

"Before the establishment of the blessed Zawiya the companions of our master [Shaykh Ahmad al-Tijani] used to congregate for the daily remembrance beside the door of his house in Fez, and occasionally in some of the city's mosques, until the Prophet ﷺ commanded our master to construct the blessed zawiya and select the best and purest land for it. He chose the location, based upon an indication from the Prophet ﷺ, in the city quarter of Dardās known today as al-Balīda. 

He purchased the location with his lawful and righteously-obtained wealth, and at that time there was a delapidated ruin upon the site, overgrown with large vines. The ruins were imposing, and no one was able to enter them alone. It has been transmitted to me from a reliable source that a sound used to be heard within the ruins from time to time as if there was a congregation making dhikr, and many of the ecstatics (majadhīb) of Fez used to incline towards that place. Before the zawiya's construction a famous majdhūb named Sidi al-Lahbi used to visit the ruin and place his ear to its door, saying to the onlookers, 'Come to this place and you too will hear the dhikr.' After the establishment of the zawiya there [Sidi al-Lahbi] took to saying in the streets, in the manner of the majadhīb, 'Fez has been protected, especially al-Dardās.' ...

When our master (ra) wished to build [the zawiya], the people of Fez came together with great hostility to prevent its construction. This matter eventually reached the honorable Amīr al-Mu'minīn Mawlay Sulayman [the Sultan of Morocco,] who forced them to accept the construction due to what he had witnessed from the miracles and wonders of our master Shaykh al-Tijani. He sent to our master a sum of money to assist in the building of the zawiya and to carry out whatever was needed. Our master returned the wealth in its entirety, saying, 'I have no need for that which you have given. The affair of this zawiya is established by God.' ...

When our master began carrying out the construction of the blessed zawiya, he ordered for a stone to be cut to a specific shape, then he engraved upon the stone the Greatest Name of Allah, writing with it, 'O Allah, I ask you by the right of Your Great and Most Majestic Name that you preserve my companions from Qāf to Qāf (i.e. wherever they may be).' Then he commanded that the stone be buried in the foundation of the blessed zawiya's wall, and it has also been said it was placed at the top of the wall. And among those who attended the burying [of the Greatest Name] was the great Muqaddam Sidi Umar, the grandson of the mighty gnostic and spiritual pole Sidi Abd al-Azīz al-Dabbagh, and others from the elite disciples of our master. It may be that the location of the Great Name is the second column to the right of the noble grave [of Shaykh al-Tijani], known to the elect as the 'Column of Gold'..."

— Translation from the Kashf al-Hijāb of Shaykh Ahmad Sukayrij (ra).
---
Construction of Zawiya in Fes:
Construction of Zawiya in Fes 

"Before the establishment of the blessed Zawiya the companions of our master [Shaykh Ahmad al-Tijani] used to congregate for the daily remembrance beside the door of his house in Fez, and occasionally in some of the city's mosques, until the Prophet ﷺ commanded our master to construct the blessed zawiya and select the best and purest land for it. Standing as the Image of Allah:
Standing as the Image of Allah

"One day, Mawlay Muhammad ibn Abi Nasr al-Alawi (may Allah profit us by him), was walking in the district of the Sharabiliyine in the city of Fez (may Allah preserve it from every harm) when he found Sidna Shaykh Abu'l Abbas Ahmad al-Tijani (may Allah be pleased with him) standing in the middle of the crossroads of Darb Zuqaq Rawah while people were looking at him from the four directions. 
So when he saw our Master (may Allah be pleased with him) he greeted him and stayed next to him until he departed with him to his residence (i.e. Dar Lamraya). There, he asked him, “Oh Master! What is the reason behind your long standing at that place?” 
Our Shaykh (may Allah be pleased with him) answered: “The Divine Presence told me, ‘Go out to My slaves in My Image. Whoever has seen you has seen
Al Rahman”
—Shaykh Ahmad Sukayrij al-Tijani (ra), Kashif al-Hijab

What makes me me? People Before Death:
What makes me me? People Before Death 

On his penultimate day, Seyyidina (may ALLAH sanctify his precious secret) asked one of his companions: “Bring me five companions to spend the night with me” but he changed his mind and specified: “I cannot do without my servant girl tonight and it is inappropriate to encourage promiscuity between men and women.”

He also asked them to bring him the poem of Imam Ghazzali (may ALLAH be pleased with him), he put it under his pillow the day before his passing as Imam Ghazzali (may ALLAH be pleased with him) had done. Here are the first verses of this poem:
Ask the brothers who have seen me dead,

Who have wept and have sorrowfully recited the funeral litany for me

Is your sorrow for he who has gone

Or for he who remains present among you

Do you truly believe that I am this corpse?

No, by God! This dead body is not me.

In this shape, this body

Was my clothes, my tunic for a while.

I am a pearl enclosed in a shell

Which was for me a prison to which I was accustomed.

I am a bird and this is my cage

I have flown and this body has stayed behind to perish

I give thanks to ALLAH who has freed me

And who has built an abode for me on high

Before today I was dead among you

I have relived and I have removed my shroud

Today I talk with the noble assemblies

And I see the truth with my own eyes.

I am standing before the well-guarded tablet

On which I read and I see

All that was, all that will be and all that is imminent
---
Ar-Rahman Established on the Throne:
Ar-Rahman Established on the Throne 

"Ar Rahman is firmly established on the Throne" (Surah Taha)

This verse is not pertaining to Allah's Essence for He didn't use any of the Attributes pertaining to the Dhat (Living, Power, Knowing, Will, Hearing, Seeing, Speaking) but He rather used an Attribute pertaining to His Sifat (Character i.e Merciful).

As for Arsh it is the symbol in creation of Allah's Power and Might for there is no creation that compares to the size and vastness of Arsh and by it all that enters existence from the Muhamadan Reality enters through it to the est of creation.

For this reason Allah has stated in the Hadith Qudsi "My Mercy (Rahma) precedes my Wrath". Its (Arsh) relation to creation is the same as the relation between the heart and the body.

-Sidina Shaykh Ahmad Tijani from the Jawahir al Ma'ani 
---
POEM SEEKING MARIFAH BY SHAYKH AHMAD TIJANI (RA):
POEM SEEKING MARIFAH BY SHAYKH AHMAD TIJANI (RA)
WILL I GET DRUNK IN YOUR LOVE  أَلاَ لَيْتَ شِعْرِي هَلْ أَفُوزُ بِسَكْرَةٍ
A poem written by Shaykh Ahmad Tijani (RA) in his youth yearning for Ma’rifah
(From: Jawahir al-Ma’ani )  

أَلاَ لَيْتَ شِعْرِي هَلْ أَفُوزُ بِسَكْرَةٍ * مِنَ الحُبِّ تُحْيِي مِنِّي كُلَّ رَمِيمَةِ
How I wonder if I will ever get drunk in Your love...
With an intoxication that will revive my dead being!

وَ هَلْ لِذُرَى الإِحْسَانِ تَرْقَى عَوَالِمِي * وَهَلْ تَتَجَلَّى الذَّاتُ فِيهَا لِفِكْرَةِ
And will my consciousness ever be elevated to the level of Ihsan…  
And will the Being of God manifest itself to me, for thought!

وَ هَلْ لِي بِغَيْبِ الغَيْبِ بِاللَّهِ غَيْبَةٌ * تُغَيِبُ كُلِّي عَنْ جَمِيعِ الخَلِيقَةِ
And will I vanish in Allah, in the depths of the Unseen!
Where my entire being is vanished from all creation!

وَ هَلْ نَفَحَاتُ الْقُرْبِ فَضْلًا تَعُمُّنِي *  وَ قَدْ هُدِمَتْ مِنِّي رُسُومُ الطَّبِيعَةِ
And will the proximity of God be granted to me…
After destroying all semblances of my carnal existence!

وَ هَلْ جَذَبَاتٌ بِالتَّجَلِّي تَعُمُّنِي * فَتَسْلُبُنِي عَنْ كُلِّ كُلِّي وَجُمْلَتِي 
And will the pulls of His Manifestation overcome me…
And deprive me of my entire being and existence?!

وَ هَلْ وَارِدَاتُ الوَصْلِ مَنًّا تُزَفُّ لِي * لِكَيْ أَرْتَقِي العَلْيَاءَ مِنْ كُلِّ رُتْبَةٍ
And will the calls of His proximity come to me…
So that I rise to the highest of levels (in Ma’rifah)!

وَ هَلْ أَرِدَنْ بَحْرَ الشُّهُودِ فَيَشْتَفِي * غَلِيلِي بِغَوْصِي فِيهِ فِي كُلِّ لَمْحَةِ
And will I drink from the Ocean of Witnessing (God)!
And quench my thirst by diving in it, in every moment!

وَ هَلْ تَطْلُعَنْ شَمْسُ المَعَارِفِ جَهْرَةً * بِبَاطِنِ قَلْبِي وَالهُدى لِيَ زُفَّتِ
And will the Sun of Divine Knowledge shine openly...
in the depths of my heart & Divine guidance be granted to it!

وَ هَلْ أَرْتَقِي عَرْشَ الحَقَائِقِ وَاصِلاً * إِلَى اللَّهِ مَحْفُوفًا بِكُلِّ كَرِيمَةِ
And will I ascend the throne of Divine Realities…
Arriving in the Presence of Allah with all honour!

وَ هَلْ حُلَّةَ التَّوْحِيدِ ألْبَسُهَا وَ قَدْ * تَمَكَّنَ سِرِّي مِنْ بِسَاطِ الحَقِيقَةِ
And will I wear the garment of (Divine) Oneness…
After establishing the realm of Reality in my innermost being!

وَ هَلْ لِي بِجَمْعِ الجَمْعِ بِاللَّهِ وَصْلَةٌ * وَ قَدْ طَلَعَتْ شَمْسُ الْوُصُولِ بِقِبْلَتِي
And will I arrive in Allah’s Presence in a moment of complete Oneness!
And the Sun of Arrival shines in my direction!

وَ هَلْ وَابِلُ العِلْمِ اللَّدُنِيِّ هَاطِلٌ * إِلَيَّ وَ يَبْقَى دَائِمًا كُلَّ لَحْظَةِ  
And will the rains of Divine Knowledge pour upon me!
And remain pouring forever and every moment!

وَ هَلْ أَمَلِي مِنْ هَذِهِ بَالِغُ المَدَى * فَيَا حَبَّذَا أَمْ لاَ بُلُوغَ لِمُنْيَتِي 
So will these desires of mine be fulfilled…? 
As I wish or will I never attain my wish!

وَ هَلْ تَجْمَعُ الأَيَّامُ شَمْلِي بِبُغْيَتِي * وَنَيْلِ مُرَادي أَمْ أَمُوتُ بِحَسْرَتِي
And will the (coming) days unite me with my goal…
Attaining my desire…or will I die in regret! 

-  الله -

Shaykh Ahmad Sukayrij (RA) writes after narrating this Poem: 
“And he (Shaykh Ahmad Tijaniرضي الله عنه) attained what he desired, and achieved from Allah what he wished for, and gained the highest rank in Ma’rifah”

A PRAYER FOR THE REMOVAL OF DIFFICULTY AND ATTRACTING PROSPERITY…:
A PRAYER FOR THE REMOVAL OF DIFFICULTY AND ATTRACTING PROSPERITY 
Prescribed by Shaykh Ahmad al-Tijani (RA)
 
-          Recite YA LATIF 129 times after Salat al-Fajr
 
-        Then recite the following Du’a immediately thereafter:

بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
 
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللهُ لَطِيفٌ بِعِبَادِهِ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَ هُوَ الْقَوِيُّ الْعَزِيزُ
Allah is Compassionate with His servants! He provides for whom He wishes
and He is the all-Powerful the Majestic!
 
بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
In the name of Allah the most Merciful the ever Merciful
 
اللَّهُمَّ يَا مُسَخِّرَ السَّمَوَاتِ السَّبْعِ وَ الْأَرْضِيْنَ وَ مَنْ فِيهنَّ وَ مَنْ عَلَيْهِنَّ
O Allah! O subjugator of the Seven Heavens and the Earths
and everyone and everything in them!
 
سَخِّرْ لِي كُلَّ شَيْءٍ مِنْ عِبَادِكَ مِمَّا فِي بَرِّكَ وَ بَحْرِكَ يَا رَبَّ الْعَالَمِينَ
Subject to me everything (in the hands) of your servants
From what is in Your land and Your sea O Lord of the Worlds!
 
حَتَّى لَا يَكُونُ فِي الْكَوْنِ شَيْءٌ مُتَحَرِّكٌ أَوْ سَاكِنٌ صَامِتٌ أَوْ نَاطِقٌ ظَاهِرٌ أَوَ بَاطِنٌ
Until there is nothing moving or still in this universe, silent or vocal, apparent or hidden
 
إِلَّا سَخَّرْتَهُ لِي وَ يَكُونُ طَوْعَ أَمْرِي بِبَرَكَةِ اِسْمِكَ اللَّطِيفِ الْمَكْنُونِ يَا اللهُ يَا حَيُّ يَا قَيُّومُ
Except that You have subjected it to me and my command, through the Grace of Your most Compassionate & Hidden Name! O Allah! O Ever-Living & Ever in-Charge!
 
إِنَّمَا أَمَرُهُ إِذَا أَرَادَ شَيْئًا أَنْ يَقُولَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ
Indeed, His Affair is such that if He wishes something, He says to it: Be and it is!
 
اللَّهُمَّ جُودُكَ دَلَّنِّي عَلَيْكَ وَ إِحْسَانُكَ قَرَّبَنِي إِلَيْكَ
O Allah! Your Generosity lead me to You! And Your Bounty brought me to You!
 
أَشْكُو إِلَيْكَ مَا لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْكَ وَ أَسْأَلُكَ مَا لَا يَعْسُرُ عَلَيْكَ
I lament to You about that which is not hidden from You
and I ask of You that which is not difficult for You!
 
إِذْ عِلْمُكَ بِحَالِي يُغْنِي عَنْ سُؤَاليِ
For Your knowledge of my condition suffices from my beseeching of You!
 
يَا مُفَرِّجًا عَنْ كُلِّ مَفْرُوجٍ كَرْبَهُ وَ مُنَجِّيهِ فَرِّجْ عَنِيّ كَرْبِي وَ مَا أَنَا فِيهِ
O Remover of calamities from those afflicted with it, and their Saviour!
Remove from me the tribulation that I am in!
 
يَا مَنْ لَيْسَ بِغَائِبٍ فَأَنْتَظِرُهُ وَ لَا بِنَائِمٍ فَأُوقِظُهُ وَ لَا بِغَافِلٍ فَأُنَبِّهُهُ
O who is not absent, that I should wait for Him or asleep that I should awaken him
Or heedless that I should beg His attention!
 
وَ لَا بِنَاسٍ فَأُذَكِّرُهُ وَ لَا بِعَاجِزٍ فَأُمْهِلَهُ
O who is not forgetful, that I should remind Him or weak that I should give Him time!
 
يَا عَالِمًا بِالْجُمْلَةِ وَ غَنِيًّا عَنِ التَّفْصِيلِ يَا سَامِعًا لِلْقَالِ وَ الْقِيْلِ
O who knows all at once and is in no need of detail!
O who knows all that is said and heard!
كَفَى عِلْمُكَ عَنِ الْمَقَالِ وَ انْقَطَعَ الرَّجَاءُ إِلَّا مِنْكَ يَا مُتَعَالُ
Your knowledge suffices from any words (from me)
And all hope is lost in anyone but You!
 
وَ خَابَتِ الْآمَالُ إِلَّا فِيكَ يَا ذَا الْجَلَالِ
For all hopes have been disappointed save in You!
 
وَ انْسَدَّتِ الطُّرُقُ إِلَّا إِلَيْكَ يَا مِفْضَالُ
And all paths have been blocked but (the path) to You O Generous One!
 
يَا اللهُ يَا سَمِيعُ يَا قَرِيبُ يَا بَصِيرُ يَا مُجِيبُ
O Allah! O All-Hearing! O Most-Near! O All-Seeing! O Who answers (our pleas)!
 
اِغْفِرْ لِي وَ ارْحَمْنِي بِرَحْمَتِكَ يَا أَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِينَ
Forgive me and have mercy on me! O Most Merciful of all!
 
وَ يَسِّرْ لِي رِزْقِي وَ سَخِّرْ لِي جَمِيعَ خَلْقِكَ
And ease for me my providence and subject to me all Your creation!
 
إِنَّكَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرُ
Indeed You have the Ability to do anything!
 
وَ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ وَ آلِهِ وَ صَحْبِهِ وَ سَلَّمَ
And may the Blessings and Salutations of Allah be upon our master Muhammad
And his Family & Companions!
 
-   آمِين -

Sheikh Tijani (ra) on: The Elevated ones of the Age| Man of the Age…:
Sheikh Tijani (ra) on: The Elevated ones of the Age| Man of the Age | Qutb | Khalifa | Khulafa 

“According to Allah’s preceding Will, the connecting assistance to His creation from the overflow of His Mercy, in every age, comes with the high elite of His creation from amongst the prophets and the truthful.  Thus, whoever flees to the living elevated special ones of his age, follows them, and seeks assistance from them will attain access to the flowing assistance from Allah [therein]. The stamp of deprivation is on whoever rejects people of his age and adheres to the words of the dead friends [of Allah] before him. His example is like one who rejects the prophet of his time and his legislation, preferring the legislation of the prophets that past before him. As a result, the stamp of disbelief is inscribed on him.”

 Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) al-Jāmiʿ, pg. 177
---
On Guarding the Secrets | Letter #6 in the Discourses:
On Guarding the Secrets | Letter #6 in the Discourses 
Shaykh Ibrahim ibn ‘Abdullah Niyas al-Kawlakhi (q.s.)

“I advise myself and all of you to have taqwa in public and in private, and to occupy yourselves with Allah to the exclusion of everything other than Him.  I advise all of you to preserve the obligations of the shari’ah and to not neglect the rights of the Lord.  Most important among them is the five daily swalah, along with safeguarding all of its prerequisite conditions, such as performing them on time and in congregation.  Be careful to safeguard and maintain the obligatory awrad of the Thariqa’ Tijaniyyah, especially the daily wazhifah, along with its condition of performing it in jama’ah.  Whosoever performs it by himself, having the ability to join the jama’ah, has not fulfilled the condition of its performance.  By this, is a person known to be a Tijani.  Whosoever does not act in accordance with what we have said is not a Tijani.  Whosoever is neglectful in this has not smelled the fragrant scent of Sufism and being a faqir. 
I advise everyone who has smelled the fragrant scent of the special tawhid al-khasw to remain silent, and to avoid the gatherings of the common folk who do not gather in obedience to Allah.  I especially warn you against speaking of tawhid al-khasw and its secrets before them.  You should know that to unveil Asrar ar-Rububiyyah to those who remain veiled is more serious in the Presence of Allah than doing what is haram. 
سُوۡرَةُ الاٴحزَاب
لَّقَدۡ كَانَ لَكُمۡ فِى رَسُولِ ٱللَّهِ أُسۡوَةٌ حَسَنَةٌ۬ لِّمَن كَانَ يَرۡجُواْ ٱللَّهَ وَٱلۡيَوۡمَ ٱلۡأَخِرَ وَذَكَرَ ٱللَّهَ كَثِيرً۬ا (٢١) 
You have, indeed, in the Messenger of Allah a beautiful pattern (of conduct) for anyone whose hope is in Allah and the Final Day, and who engages much in the praise of Allah. (Surah al-Ahzab:21) 
You also have a good example to follow in our Shaykh Ahmad at-Tijani (q.s.) who used to conceal the secrets, and who used to frequently recite a poem which says, “With me, the secret is locked in a house whose key has been lost and whose doors are shut!  Do not give the secret except to one who has your full confidence, for to most people the secret is not suitable.’  He also used to say, ‘The unrestrained breast is the graveyard of the secrets.’  You also have a good example to follow in the writer of this letter, the poor and despicable servant of Allah, who has possessed this knowledge for a long time and you never heard any mention, or indication of it from me, which would single me out among my neighbours or loved ones, until the Command of Allah came to me.  I thank and praise Allah for that, because we are the chiefs among the Malamatiyyah and our way is to conceal our spiritual station and our miraculous feats. 
The Malamatiyyah draw no special attention to themselves and each one is engaged in his trade or work.  They make no claim of laudable advantage over the common folk, nor do they unveil their performance of miracles or their knowledge of the unseen, as that is considered the menstruation of men.  We are concerned with the unveiling of light, not the unveiling of darkness.  Our sign of miracles are to be found in our hearts and not on the horizons, as we are the inheritors of Muhammad (s.a.w.), and the Muhammadan inheritance are the miracles of the heart, which in the constant increase of knowledge, spiritual states, and experiential tasting with the passing of every breath.  This is alluded to in the Saying of the Most High: 
سُوۡرَةُ حٰمٓ السجدة / فُصّلَت
سَنُرِيهِمۡ ءَايَـٰتِنَا فِى ٱلۡأَفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِہِمۡ حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمۡ أَنَّهُ ٱلۡحَقُّ‌ۗ أَوَلَمۡ يَكۡفِ بِرَبِّكَ أَنَّهُ ۥ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَىۡءٍ۬ شَہِيدٌ (٥٣) 
Soon will We show them Our Signs in the (furthest) regions (of the Earth), and in their own souls until it becomes manifest to them that this is the Truth.  Is it not enough that thy Lord does Witness all things? (Surah Fuswswilat:53) 
You should know that I am free and clear of every spiritually enraptured person who does not continue to travel the path as a salik.  To speak to people before permission is your apparent and clear destruction, and it is the evidence of your false claim.  The servant who has witnessed the Real and His Oneness does not speak about it, nor does he point out his own annihilation.  The spiritually enraptured person who speaks does not gain anything by way of increase, and I will not assist him in his disobedience of Allah. 
The love of appearance will only prevent you from coming before the people, and I am the servant of the Divine Presence, al-Hamdulillah, and no one can take anything away from me, nor do I have a need for any reward or thanks from anyone.  The Reward I seek is that you become completely devoted to Allah, for Allah, and by Allah, without ever turning aside to follow your whims, fancies, and passions.  Your speaking to others before receiving permission is your following foul passions and ego. 
سُوۡرَةُ البَقَرَة
… فَتُوبُوٓاْ إِلَىٰ بَارِٮِٕكُمۡ فَٱقۡتُلُوٓاْ أَنفُسَكُمۡ ذَٲلِكُمۡ خَيۡرٌ۬ لَّكُمۡ عِندَ بَارِٮِٕكُمۡ … (٥٤) 
… “… so turn (in repentance) to your Maker and slay yourselves (the wrong-doers); that will be better for you in the sight of your Maker.” ... (Surah al-Baqarah:54) 
I pray that Allah gather all of our hearts in the perfection of His Gnosis and that He guide and protect us all!  Salaam.”

Shaikh at Tijani on the relationships (an nisb) & Ahadiyya::
Shaikh at Tijani on the relationships (an nisb) & Ahadiyya: 

“Know that the “unique presence” (hadrat al ahadiyya) is the first relationship emerging from the essence of the Essence (ayn adh dhat) because the Truth in the presence of Its Essence knows no relationship (nisba). The presence of the Naive Essence (adh dhat as saadhij) (348) is the ocean of blindness (bahr al a’maa), oblivion (at tams). No attribute, name, essence, trace, otherness, imagination, quantification, qualification, jurisdiction, or property can be thought of in It. When Its Essence emerges It is categorical to every consideration. Thus, no relationship can be intellected for It. The manifestations of relationships are located after departing from Essential naïveté. 
[Kitab al jami 347]

New Note:
￼
Elevated Ones the Age

“According to Allah’s preceding Will, the connecting assistance to His creation from the overflow of His Mercy, in every age, comes with the high elite of His creation from amongst the prophets and the truthful.  Thus, whoever flees to the living elevated special ones of his age, follows them, and seeks assistance from them will attain access to the flowing assistance from Allah [therein]. The stamp of deprivation is on whoever rejects people of his age and adheres to the words of the dead friends [of Allah] before him. His example is like one who rejects the prophet of his time and his legislation, preferring the legislation of the prophets that past before him. As a result, the stamp of disbelief is inscribed on him.”

 Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) al-Jāmiʿ, pg. 177

Al Mishri On the Nafs:
Al Mishri On the Nafs 
So the [human] self (al-nafs) is something whose ruling (ḥukm) exists but not its essence, as it is formed between the meeting of the soul (al-rūḥ) and the body (al-jasad). If they were to separate, it, meaning the self, which is a subtle vapor, ceases to exist. This thing called ‘the self’ is the source of reprehensible morals and corrupt sickly attributes. As long as its ruling controls the servant, the soul is captive in his hand. It does not seek anything but his pleasure which is his ultimate destruction, far from the Divine Presence based [therein] upon the power of the luminous soul (al-rūḥ). Due to its settlement in the body the soul is stained with its dirt and the rule of the evil soul seized it and it became a sinner against the command of his Lord. This is the effect of the rule of the body as the body is formed in the place of darkness which is water and dust, and it was extremely dense. (al-Mishry 2013, 84)

al-Mishry, Muḥammad bin. 2013. Rawḍ al-muḥib al-fānī fimā talaqaynā min Sīdī Abī al-ʿAbbās aṭ-Ṭijānī. Beirut: Lebanon.

Yet, Shaikh Ibrahim (ra) said, 

“The people of the Fire will be in extreme anger towards themselves, to the extent that if they had the power, they would kill themselves because it is the self (al-nafs) that committed the deeds that led them to the Fire.”

Muhammadan Reality and Knowledge of the Prophet ﷺ:
Muhammadan Reality and Knowledge of the Prophet ﷺ 

_*From the Jawahir al-Ma'ani of Sidi Ali Harazim*_ 

*I (Ali Harazim) asked him (Shaykh Ahmad Tijani) about the meaning of Allah's words (Exalted is He) about the Prophet (may Allah bless him and give him peace):*

*{You did not know what is the Book or [what is] faith} [al-Shura, 52]*

*"How do we reconcile these verses and hadiths with knowledge of the fact that the sciences of the first and the last were carried in his honored essence, and that he is the link that causes that knowledge to reach each creation according to its capacity?"*

He (Shaykh Ahmad Tijani) responded:

“You should know that the Prophet (may Allah bless him and give him peace) knew the sciences of the first and the last, absolutely and comprehensively. Among those sciences is knowledge of all Heavenly Books- let alone only the Qur’an, the demands of faith- its beginning and end, and the essence of faith, what spoils it and what strengthens it. All of that is firmly entrenched in the Muhammadan Reality (may Allah bless him and give him peace). As for His words (Blessed and Exalted),

[You did not know what is the Book or [what is] faith]

he was in this state before his Prophethood. Allah had informed him neither of the reality of faith, nor of the method of the revelation of the Heavenly Books, neither the essence of Messengerhood, nor the details of its requisites. Allah had veiled him from all of that before his Prophethood. It was hidden in his Muhammadan Reality. But he did not know it, nor did he perceive it, until when it came time for his Prophethood, Allah lifted the veils from him and he saw what his Muhammadan Reality contained. The proof of that is in his words (may Allah bless him and give him peace):

“I saw my Lord in the form of a youth,” until he said, “He placed His hand upon my shoulder blade until I felt its coldness upon between my two breasts. And he taught me the sciences of the first and the last.” (Tirmidhi, Ahmad).

That was at the time of his Prophethood. Allah lifted the veils from him and showed him the gnosis, sciences and secrets- whose seas have no shore, and which have no limit- that Allah had incorporated for him in his Muhammadan Reality. But beware of understanding from this, that the Muhammadan Reality lacked that before Prophethood. That assumption is not correct.

The Muhammadan Reality had been filled with all of those gnosis, sciences and secrets from the beginning of existence, since it is the first existent thing. Allah brought it into existence before anything else. And He endowed it with those sciences, gnosis and secrets. And it remained filled with them until the time came for his blessed body to exist (may Allah bless him and give him peace). Then a veil was placed between him and knowledge of that until the time came for his Prophethood. At that time, He (Allah) lifted the veil and showed him those aforementioned things that He had stored in his Muhammadan Reality. And His address to him in His words:

{You did not know what is the Book or [what is] faith},

I was only informing him of the state of being veiled from the knowledge that existed before in His Reality (may Allah bless him and give him peace). It was not stating that knowledge of those things was not in his reality......

And he had always been (may Allah bless him and give him peace), before his Prophethood, from the time he exited from his mother’s womb, among the greatest Knowers of God. And the veil of humanhood had not been cast over him to the degree that it would intervene between him and between knowing the Holy Divine Presence. And he was among the “Fard” saints of the world. The likeness of “Fard” saint to the ordinary Knowers of God and the “Siddīqin” is that of the Knower of God to the ordinary people who have no ma’rifa...

He (May Allah bless him and give him peace) had been established in that station to such a degree as to take knowledge from Allah without an intermediary. And he was not ignorant of any of the states of the Divine Presence. Nor did his sun (may Allah bless him and give him peace) set at that place. In that sphere, Allah had only veiled him from the essence of Messengerhood, its requirements, and those things which would have explained to him what its purpose was. And Allah had also veiled him from the method of the revelation of the Heavenly Books and those things which would have explained to him their purpose and what matters were sought through the revelation of a Heavenly Book. This was his state until he reached the level of Prophethood. At that time, the veils were lifted between his knowledge and that which had been stored in his Muhammadan Reality of sciences, gnosis and secrets......

And the secret in the draping of the veil over the Prophet (may Allah bless him and give him peace) is that if Allah had unveiled to him, before his Prophethood, what He had stored away in his Muhammadan Reality, and he had spoken about it before his Messengerhood and being dispatched, doubt about the Message that he spoke to them about would have arisen in those to whom he was sent. They would have said, “You’ve been speaking about these things all of your life. You have transmitted from someone else. And you are not a Prophet.” So Allah hid it from him so that he may not speak about it. Then, when it came time for his Prophethood, Allah lifted the veils from him. And those matters that Allah showed people about him (may Allah bless him and give him peace) before his Prophethood, such as being an uneducated person, not knowing anything and not perceiving anything, nor his mixing with or becoming close with any of the People of the Book, were so that when he spoke to them about matters of Messengerhood and Prophethood, they would know that it is the truth. That is because it came from an uneducated person who had not known anything. And that could only happen by Prophethood. And that is the secret of his being veiled. Proof of this is in His words (Blessed and Exalted):

{And you did not recite before it any scripture, nor did you inscribe one with your right hand} [al-Ankabut, 48].

.....And from the greatest evidences of what we have mentioned about him (may Allah bless him and give him peace) is that his state before his Prophethood - the sciences of his Prophethood, Messengerhood, Heavenly Books and of Faith being existent in his reality, but hidden from him by a veil - is like that of a sleeping person. Those sciences which he knew while he was awake are hidden from him at the time of sleep. And that is the case until when he wakes up, and the veil of sleep is lifted from him, he connects with it and finds that they remained in his essence. That was his state (may Allah bless him and give him peace) from the time his body was created until his Prophethood.”
---
Shaikh Aḥmad at-Tijānī (ra) on The Reality of the Human Being (Ḥaqīqat…:
Shaikh Aḥmad at-Tijānī (ra) on The Reality of the Human Being (Ḥaqīqat al-insān)

‘...in reality, the human being is a combination of the soul (al-rūḥ) and the body (al-jism). Neither of them holds tyranny over the other in his reality. Allah (t.a.) only mentions human’s reality in terms of his body like His saying (t.a.): ‘and we certainly did We create man from an extract of clay ’ (23:12) (pg.89) and like His saying (t.a.): ‘Recite in the name of your Lord who created (96:1) and elsewhere in the Qurānic signs. Thus, whenever He mentions the human’s creation he only mentions the form of his body. The affair of the soul has been concealed by Allah and kept away from creation and only known to Him. When the question about it arose He said: ‘ The soul is of the affair of my Lord….’ (17:85) He did not explain it any further due to His keeping its knowledge to Himself (t.a.). The above is the outward reality of the human being.
The inner reality of the human being is indicated in his words (s.a.w.s.): ‘ Allah created Adam on His form.’ He indicated a subtle point in this [and that is that] the human being is the presence of perfection (ḥaḍrat al-kamāl) met by the presence of beauty (ḥaḍrat al-jamāl) encompassing the entire divine secret. Shaikh al-Akbar said in the Openings (al-futuḥāt): ‘What is Adam’s attribute? He said: ‘If you wish you can say the form of the divine presence or if you wish you [could also have] said: ‘The totality of the divine names….’ (Al-Mishry 2018, 89-90)
Al-Mishry, Muḥammad ibn. 2018. Rawḍ al-muḥib al-fānī fī mā talaqqaynāhu min Sīdī Abī al-ʿAbbās at-Tijānī (Beirut: Dār al-kutub al-ʿilmiyya).

100 Salatul Fatih at Night:
100 Salatul Fatih at Night 

Sidi Ahmed al-Tijani, may Allah be pleased with him and make him pleased, said: ‘Reciting one hundred of the Salat al-Fatih prayer on the night of Friday, after people have gone to sleep, atones for four hundred years.’”

This is sourced from the book “Al-Ifadah al-Ahmadiyya”.

On Merit Being Based on the One Followed:
On Merit Being Based on the One Followed
Sheikh Tijani (may ALLAH be pleased with him and sanctify his precious secret) asked the Prophet ﷺ what was the reason for all the merits and the blessings contained in this path, and the Prophet ﷺ answered: “It is because of you”. The Prophet also said: “You are the door to success for all the disobedient that are connected to you.” (Djawahiru-l-Ma’ani)

Similarly, Sheikh Omar Futi (ra) said: “The merit that is granted to those who follow relies entirely on the merit that is held by he who is followed.” (Rimah)

Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) on the Man of the Age is the Same as Existence…:
Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) on the Man of the Age is the Same as Existence and the Nature of His Soul and Will

According to Muḥammad al-Mishry (ra), Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) was asked about the following verses. 
'I have been hidden from my age by His Presence.
So I began to see my age, and they did not see me.
If you asked the days my name is, they would not know
what or where my location is.' (al-Mishrī, n.d., 208)
al-Mishry writes:
"He answered (r.a.a.) that [verses above reference] the level of the Greatest Vicegerent (al-khalīfa al-ʿatham) as no name specifies him for the names of existence are all his names due to his having realized their levels and for his being the Soul (al-rūḥ) in all existent entities (al-mawjūdāt). There is no essence in existence, but it is the determining soul (al-rūḥ al-mudabbar), its mover (al-muḥarrik), and that which exists (al-qāʿim) in it. There is no place in the sphere of the world but that he is firmly situated therein. In this sense, no name distinguishes him from existence. There is no place specific to him over another. This is why he said:’ If you asked the days…
He is indicating the level of the Greatest Vicegerent. Al-Mursī said: ‘If the Friend's reality were revealed, he would be worshipped instead of Allah because his attributes are from His Attributes and features from His Features. ‘Friend’ means the Complete Human (al-insān al-kāmil); he is the Greatest Vicegerent. This is the meaning of His words (t.a.):. ‘and is one who was dead, and We gave him light [by which to walk among the people like one who is in darkness, never to emerge from that place?..] (6:122) (al-Mishrī, n.d., 208)
Muḥyiddīn said that the human being veiled from Allah is not a human. Instead, he resembles the human as the dead who have no soul. It is a human essence, but it has no soul. When the Sufis say that the soul is uncreated, rather it is pre-eternal (qadīma azaliyya), they are indicating this soul [meaning that present in the Greatest Vicegerent above], which is the purity of experiential knowledge (ṣafāʿ al-maʿarifa) after the opening. The one who has it does as he wills in whatever [matter] he wills. He revives the dead. If he wills, he calls upon him, and he [i.e., the dead] responds [to him] immediately even if he were dust. Dry stones produce fruit instantly if he wants, amongst other miracles. No miracle is difficult for him, but the mountain of etiquette with the Divine Presence prevents him from performing them.
Suppose he manifests a miracle as per the moment’s requirement. In that case, he is immediately punished, abandoned, or deprived because he is erased in the Divine Presence and dead to all his [selfish] portions. He does not carry out the Truth’s undertakings. If it was said to him, ‘what do you want?’ He would say: ‘I only want what the Truth (s.w.t.) wants. He is annihilated from his own will." (al-Mishrī, n.d., 208–209)
Mishrī, Muḥammad al-. n.d. Al-Jāmiʿ Li Durar Al-ʿulūm Al-Fāʿiḍa Min Buḥūr Al-Quṭb Al-Maktūm. Edited by Muḥammad Al-Rāḍī Kannūn. Rabat: Dār al-imān.

Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) on The Reality of the Complete Human (ḥaqīqat…:
Shaikh al-Tijānī (ra) on The Reality of the Complete Human (ḥaqīqat al-insān al-kāmil)

“I asked him (r.a.) about the reality of the Complete Human. He responded (r.a.): ‘The reality of the Complete Human is the presence of perfection (kamāl) which met with the presence of beauty (jamāl) which contained the entire divine secret who, from this point, was Allah’s successor over existence (khalīfa Allāh ʿalā al-wujūd). Whereas the Lord is a god, the human is a ruler, disposing within that which is divined over. Every plane (martaba) of the Lord has a divinity on it, and the [Complete] Human has disposal (taṣarruf), judgment (ḥukm), and succession (khilāfa) over it. His ruling over it is not prevented in any way.
Allah ordered the angels to prostrate to Adam for this reason. It is symbolized by his saying (s.a.w.s.): ‘Allah created Adam in his image.’ The Complete Human is he who attains this plane and whoever does not have this rank has none of its benefits. Rather he resembles the Human but is not the Human. Instead, he is a soulless dead man. He looks like a dead person, motionless and lifeless. He does not have the characteristics of a human due to his being dead for the qualities of humanity follow his life. Dead people do not possess human characteristics.
As for the [statement] ‘ contained the entire divine secret’ [means] he did not contain any of the Divine Names except those upon which the existence of the universe depends. As for the Names that do not involve the universe, the [Complete] Human only knows them through the path of emanation without his realizing their [onto-epistemic] end. They have no end, and people are only acquainted with them as per the divine portion [assigned to them], [be it] small or great. Peace.
What is meant by the ‘reality of the Complete Human’ (al-insān al-kāmil) is when Allah manifests to the slave He causes him to die a true death and destroys him. He has no remaining sense, feeling, understanding, knowledge, or name. Other and otherness faded away epistemologically (ʿilman), cognitively (fahman), sensorily (iḥsāsan), perceptively (idrākan), as a realization (taḥaqquqan), and relationship (taʿalluqan). Nothing remains but Truth, alone. There the slave is donned with noble garments and serious and severe suits with from the Divine Attributes (al-awṣāf al-ilāhiyya) and spirituality (al-ruḥāniyya). He returns to existence through an existence other than his original existence. Thus, his [ontological] extent and measure is unknown. (pg.36)
The above is the reality of the Complete Human. To this is the indication of His words (t.w.t.): ‘ and is one who as dead and We gave him life…’ (6:122), as well as his words (s.a.w.s.): ‘ People are asleep and when they die they awaken,’ [as per] the prophetic tradition (al-ḥadīth), and his words (a.s.s.): ‘whoever would like to see a dead [man] walking on the face of the earth then let him look at Abū Bakr aṣ-Ṣiddīq,’ [as per] the prophetic tradition. (Al-Mishry 2018, 36-37)
It has been narrated from Muḥammad ibn ʿAlī ibn Abī Ṭālib (r.a.a.) [that the latter] said: ‘Allah looks into creation three hundred and sixty times a day.’ These glances are all through the eye of supervision. These glances mean the blessing they grant and the effulgences they overflow from the treasures of His grace. The word "look" is used metaphorically.
The place of Allah’s glance (t.w.t.) in the earth is the meadow containing his body (s.a.w.s.) and the Honorable Kabah, as the Complete Human is the site of Allah’s gaze (t.w.t.) in the world in his time, as he (s.a.w.s.) is the site of Allah’s gaze (t.w.t.) in all of existence from pre-eternity to post-eternity. (Al-Mishry 2018, 307)
The [Complete] Human’s Carrying the Trust
He was asked (r.a.a.) about the meaning of His words (t.a.): ‘Indeed we offered the Trust to the heavens and earth…’ (33:72) etc., He answered: ‘The Trust is to establish the rights of the Truth in all its meanings to do with creation and divinity. The heavens and earth could not bear the burden of Trust and declined it. The human took on the burden. He is the Complete Human on account of whom Allah protects the system of existence (niẓām al-wujūd), He shows mercy through him. All of him is existence (jamīʿahu=[ al-wujūd). All existence is rectified through him. He is the life (pg.325) of all of existence. All life is carried out through him. Were he to non-exist (zāla ʿan al-wujūd) for [even] for single blinking of the eye all of the existence would become non-existence in the blinking of an eye (i.e., instantaneously). Common folk refer to him as the Pole of Poles (quṭb al-aqṭāb), and the Universal Aid (al-ġawṯ al-jāmiʿ).
His words: ‘unjust and ignorant’ do not mean that he was unjust because he crossed humanity and nature's limits nor traversed into the domain of truth, wherein there is no location, qualification, form, nor limit. No one but Allah alone can do that. (Rather) the meaning of his unjustness is his transcending the limits of the plane of humanity and creation for he is incapable of exceed the affair [he exceeds]. It is impossible to encompass the affair he has crossed since it has no zenith nor end. He said (s.w.t.): ‘ but they do not encompass it in knowledge.’ This is the meaning of the ignorance [mentioned above]. The unjustness that is attributed to him is according to the planes the Truth chose for his slave.
The ignorance attributed to him [as mentioned above] is a negation of the comprehension of the essence of the essence (kunh al-ḏāt) of His Sublimity (jalālihi). That is the fullest extent of the experiential knowledge (al-maʿarifa) of Allah. His experiential knowledge of Allah is entirely beyond these two lines, meaning the scope (dāʿira) of the state of loyalty (dāʿirat aṣ-ṣidīqiyya) and that all the experiential knowledge belonging to the people of loyalty (aṣ-ṣiddiqqīn) has a relative scope. This scope’s limitations and fullest extent cannot be traversed. The Complete Human has traversed every scope and arrived at the experiential knowledge of Allah through Allah where there is no encompassment of the extent of His Sublimity (kunh jalālihi), nor limit, trace, qualification, or scope. He patrols this ocean without limit even if all existent things (al-mawjūdāt) extend from this ocean." (Al-Mishry 2018, 326)
Al-Mishry, Muḥammad ibn. 2018. Rawḍ al-muḥib al-fānī fī mā talaqqaynāhu min Sīdī Abī al-ʿAbbī al-ʿAbbās al-Tijānī (Beirut: Dār al-kutub al-ʿilmiyya).

And Allah Warns You of His Self:
And Allah Warns You of His Self

“Our Shaikh (r.a.) was asked about His words (t.a.): ‘...and Allah warns you of His Self (nafs).’ (3:28)
He answered (r.a.): ‘Its legal application is that He warns you of His Self by being scared of His scheming throughout all the blessings He gave you and to ward off any vengeful harm that could come your way in that condition. No one feels secure from Allah’s deception but those who deserve the torment of the Majestic.
In terms of [its meaning] within the Reality [of]  ‘...and Allah warns you of His Self (nafs).’ (3:28)
From researching, investigating, and asking about the essence of the essence (kunh al-ḏāt). It is not appropriate for you as you do not have the capacity required for that affair. Thus, beware calamities’ descent upon you for inquiry about that affair. Restrain yourselves in keeping with the Lawgiver's command (s.a.w.s.).’ “  (Al-Mishry 2018, 328)
Al-Mishry, Muḥammad ibn. 2018. Rawḍ al-muḥib al-fānī fī mā talaqqaynāhu min Sīdī Abī al-ʿAbbī al-ʿAbbās al-Tijānī (Beirut: Dār al-kutub al-ʿilmiyya).

Huwa:
Huwa 

“I was pushed forward by a burst (dufʿa) from the divine presence. My beginning became my end, my end my beginning. My entirety became my every particle, and my every particle became my entirety. I became Him, and He me, but as becoming of Him, and not as becoming of me. At that moment, if I were asked a million separate ques- tions, I would have given only one answer. Then I became like the niche of light (miṣbāḥ).” Shaykh al-Islām Ibrāhīm Niasse was attached to this statement, saying, “These words are the reason for my being pleased to have him as our shaykh.”

On the Spirit and Body:
On the Spirit and Body 

“God created realization [ma’rifa] when He joined the spirit with the body, then He called it a human being, and addressed it.” [Muḥammad b. al-Mishrī, al-Jāmiʿ li-durar al-ʿulūm al-fāʾiḍa min biḥār al-quṭb al-maktūm (printed manuscript, Rabat: Muḥammad Rāḍī Kanūn, 2002), 1:101.]

The Translated and Structured Tijani Istikhara ::
The Translated and Structured Tijani Istikhara :

1. Begin by performing ablution (wudu) to purify yourself.

2. Stand to perform two rak'ahs of prayer (non-obligatory prayer). In each rak'ah, after Surah Al-Fatiha, recite Surah Al-Kafirun in the first rak'ah, and Surah Al-Ikhlas in the second rak'ah.

3. Once you complete your prayer with salam (the closing of the prayer), sit and recite Surah Al-Fatiha once.

4. Then, recite Surah Al-Ikhlas once.

5. Now, recite the well-known Istikharah supplication from the books of Hadith, ending with "then make me satisfied with it".

6. Once you've finished the supplication, recite Surah Al-Fatiha once.

7. Repeat the process of supplication and recitation of Surah Al-Fatiha until you've completed it seven times. Each round of supplication should end with Surah Al-Fatiha.

8. After the seventh round, recite Surah Al-Ikhlas three times.

9. Now, perform the two rak'ahs of prayer again, as described in step 2.

10. Repeat the entire process (steps 3 to 10) two more times.

The Istikharah supplication is as follows:

"O Allah, I seek Your guidance [in making a choice] by virtue of Your knowledge, and I seek ability by virtue of Your power, and I ask You of Your great bounty. You have power, I have none. And You know, I know not. You are the Knower of hidden things. O Allah, if in Your knowledge, this matter is good for my religion, my livelihood and my affairs (or said: for me both in this world and the next), then ordain it for me, make it easy for me, and bless it for me. And if in Your knowledge, this matter is bad for my religion, my livelihood and my affairs (or said: for me both in this world and the next), then turn it away from me, and turn me away from it. And ordain for me the good wherever it may be and make me pleased with it."

During the supplication, make sure to mention your specific need or the matter about which you are seeking guidance.
￼

Shaikh al-Tijani (ra) said in al-Jaami’ pg: 172::
Shaikh al-Tijani (ra) said in al-Jaami’ pg: 172:

“As for the question of whether the brothers of our master Joseph, peace be upon them, were prophets or not, the answer is that they were prophets, based on His saying, glory be to Him: 

'We have revealed to you, as We revealed to Noah and the Prophets after him...and to the Tribes,' and the Tribes are the children of Jacob, peace be upon him. (4:163)”

(Each tribe is produced by a son of Jacob thus they received revelation)

“As for the oneness of Allah in reality, it is His oneness in His…:
“As for the oneness of Allah in reality, it is His oneness in His Essence, and this guarantees His Oneness in His actions and attributes, and the opposite is incorrect. Whoever denies a partner with Allah (t.a.), meaning that he denies the existence of a god with Allah, rather he denies the existence of anything with Allah according to his saying: ‘And worship Allah and do not associate a partner with Him’ (4:36) then he has unified Allah. And the first thing that must be denied is the pronoun of the subject- the unifer of monotheism, so there is no subject with Allah and nothing exists with Him. Shaikh Aḥmad at-Tijānī (r.a.): ‘As long as you perceive that you are the unifier and that Allah is the unified there are two [existents]. Where is the unification [in that case]? There is no unity unless the unification is through Allah, from Allah, and to Allah. The slave has no entryway [to it] nor exit [from it]. [This experience] is not authentic outside the path of annihilation. If the monotheist sees the signs of Allah in the horizons and does not see anyone but Allah, and is shown the signs of Allah in himself, and he does not see a seer or a visible one, then Allah has been united and it becomes clear that He is the Truth. (41:53) His words (t.a.): ‘We will show them” is not idle, meaning that Allah (t.w.t.) overcomes every aspect of the slave until he does not register vision, nor any intermediary remains nor intermediator. Allah alone is the actor. If any aspect of the seer remained, he would naturally be the seer. However, the verse, in a way that is appropriate [states]: ‘We will show him Our signs.’ However, in actuality, the Seer and the Seen are Allah. (Ash-Shaikh 2012a, 226)
---
[The distinctions between essence and accidents is only mental but…:
[The distinctions between essence and accidents is only mental but otherwise unreal]:

It was said to Sayyidinā (i.e., Shaikh at-Tijānī), may God be pleased with him, 
‘Perception (idrāk) is one of the meanings. It is not an essence (jawhar) that can be decided upon.’ He said: ‘That [definition] is with regard to the limited intellect. As for its relationship to God, the realities (al-haqaaiq), their essences and accidents are all the same. This is as it has come in the tradition about the forms of actions in the grave and what is afterward regarding the states of the hereafter all of which cannot be denied. If this has been affirmed then there is no difference in the discourse of the realities regarding essence or accident. Kitab al jaam’i pg 251
---
Shaikh at-Tijānī on the Oneness of Existence (waḥadat al-wujūd) includes…:
Shaikh at-Tijānī on the Oneness of Existence (waḥadat al-wujūd) includes its bifurcations (iftirāq):

“It is only the relationships of existence that differ according to the manner in which the Will of the Truth has divided them within it between the honored and the inferior, elevated and suppressed, despised and (243) precious, the celebrated and the despicable, until the final relationship in it. The relationship’s separations do not remove them from its single essentiality. This is similar to the human essence. Its unity does not negate the different relationships of its parts and the particulars of each part in its properties. The hand’s properties are not like that of the foot. Their properties are not like that of the eye. All properties, limbs, and parts are like this. His honor’s raising in the epitome of respect, and the loveless of his position in the epitome of loss and insult does not remove him from his essence’s unity despite all the varying specifics. The same is said regarding the oneness of existence. Its unity does not remove it from its having various parts and specifics as we have said regarding the human’s essence. ( al-Mishrī 2013, 245) 

He used ink to exemplify his intentions stating:

“....The various letters are contained in the ink and the miscellaneous words and various meanings the forms of the ink indicate do not remove it from the unity of its inkness. There is nothing there but ink formed in their shapes indicating different meanings, and individual letters, miscellaneous properties are neither recombinant nor similar. Were you to look at the essence of these forms whose letters and words differ you only see ink manifesting in their forms but they are just ink. They unit in inkness and differ in form, shape, words, and meanings. 
Just as the ink in those letters is their essence, and the letters in that ink are the essence of that ink and they are composed of varying shapes, secrets, properties and meanings ad nauseum. Likewise, existence in the essences of existence is the essence of those essences. 

Those essences in that existence are the essence of that existence. They are also of various shapes varying shapes, secrets, properties and meanings. Its unity in the essence of that existence does not remove it from the difference of its shapes, secrets, meanings, and properties. Nor does its bifurcation (iftirāq) via those secrets, properties, and meanings remove it from the oneness of that existence as it is with letters and ink. Likewise the unity of the ink does not remove it from the difference of its forms, secrets, meanings, and properties. Nor dor does its bifurcation in these affairs remove it from its unity in that ink. [...] The truth (of the matter) has been made clear for the one who understood.” ( al-Mishrī 2013, 245) 



al-Mishry, Muḥammad bin. 2013. Rawḍ al-muḥib al-fānī fimā talaqaynā min Sīdī Abī al-ʿAbbās aṭ-Ṭijānī. Beirut: Lebanon.
---
For al-Tijānī, adab on the Sufi path meant a singularity of purpose…:
For al-Tijānī, adab on the Sufi path meant a singularity of purpose: acquiring a disposition of “divine adoration and the exaltation of divinity.” Having mastered this state, the shaykh allegedly refrained from asking God for anything. According to Ḥarāzim, al-Tijānī said, “I only supplicate (God) with my tongue, my heart remains submitted to (the decree of) God. I do not desire anything, and I do not ask for anything.”147 

Of course, such contentment with divine decree only increased God’s favor. In explanation, Ibrāhīm Niasse cited God’s statement to the Prophet in ḥadīth qudsī: “Whoever is too occupied with the Qurʾān and my remembrance from asking anything from Me, I give him more than is given the petitioners.”148 

Although al-Tijānī did seek spiritual stations of ultimate proximity to God, he echoed al-Kurdī in warning against asking God for saintly ranks for their own sake. “The perfected saints,” al-Tijānī warned, “do not ask for spiritual rank (maqām), and they are indistinguishable from others.”149 In explaining different types of “idolatry of purpose” (shirk al-aghrāḍ), al- Tijānī thus remonstrated: “Sincerity with the gnostics is to worship God for His own sake alone, anything else is idolatry of purpose.”150
The state of ultimate contentment with God depended on the enduring Sufi concept of self-purification (tazkiyat al-nafs). Although al-Tijānī’s teachings deemphasized earlier Sufi understandings of worldly asceticism (zuhd) and isolation (khalwa), he himself practiced periodic spiritual retreats, restricted his diet, and carried himself with such humility that he could not be distinguished from his students.
---

Shaikh al-Tijani (r.a.) said: “Spending time with those who hate (the Shaikh) is a poison that runs through the one who does so.”

In other words, avoid those who hate your Shaikh otherwise you will also begin to hate your Shaikh.

Our path is based in pure grace. The Prophet (s.a.a.w.s) gave it to me directly without any intermediaries, while I was awake, not asleep.

If all the spiritual poles of this community were to be gathered together they would not outweigh a single hair of the ocean (of virtue) of any one individual from amongst a group of my companions.

Every Shaikh, from the time of the Companions until the blowing of the horn (signalling the Day of Judgement) is taking (their everything) from me.

“Allah (t.w.t.) gives us and our companions more than 100,000 times over that which He gives to (any)one who does an accepted act, be it an obligatory or voluntary while we (ourselves) are asleep/resting.” Shaikh al-Tijani (r.a.a.)

The human essence (being) encompasses all existents (muḥīṭah bi jamīʿ…:
The human essence (being) encompasses all existents (muḥīṭah bi jamīʿ al-mawjūdāt). The reality of every ʿārif is al-Iḥāṭah (the encompassment) of all the angels and all existent things from the throne to the floor. He sees all of it in his essence (being), one by one, to the extent that if he wanted to look into the unseen onto the tablet (al-lawḥ) he would look into his essence (being) and investigate it. This perfection is only for humans. For this reason common complete vicegerency of Allah's is made in him (human) for this encompassment.  

-Shaikh al-Tijani, Kitāb al-Jāmiʿ, 674.

Toward the end of his life, some visitors asked Shaykh Aḥmad al-Tijānī…:
Toward the end of his life, some visitors asked Shaykh Aḥmad al-Tijānī, “If your companions have been given what has not been given the greatest axial saints (aqṭāb), where does that leave you?”
He responded, “I am nothing but a poor man (miskīn).”1 

As a manifestation of divine favor rather than individual merit, Islamic sainthood never set itself in opposition to human frailty. Claims to high spiritual rank are thus not inconsistent with the humility inseparable from the human condition, reflecting divine bestowal rather than personal ascription.

 “The meaning of miskīn,” al-Tijānī explained, “is contained in the Prophet’s words, ‘O God, raise me among the needy (iḥyanī miskīnan).’ It is the locus of God’s gaze in His creation.”

As the focus of divine “gaze,” the saint and his claims were not to be taken lightly. Al-Tijānī warned his contemporaries:

 “We do not take the sanctity (ḥurma) of our saintly masters lightly, and we are not negligent in venerating them. Whoever venerates the sanctity of the saints, both alive and dead, God will exalt his own sanctity. Whoever disparages them, God humiliates him and is angry with him. We do not overlook the sanctity of the saints.”3

Z. Wright, Realising Islam, pg. 142,  2020

Shaikh Tijani—The yearning of the soul::
Shaikh Tijani—The yearning of the soul: 

God created the [human] spirit 980,000 years in length, and the same in width. And He left it a long time in His nurturing care, caressing it in the tenderness of His kindness, of His graciousness, of the manifest traces of His love for it. And the spirit grew strong in this nurturing care. Then when it tasted the pain of separation, it cried out in complaint, and said, “O my God, my Master and Lord, I cannot endure this separation!” And its Lord said to it, may He be glorified and exalted,

 “I did not create you to desire yourself, I created you to manifest in you the secret of My oneness (waḥdāniyya).”

On Whether the Patient Pauper or the Grateful Rich Person is Superior:

On Whether the Patient Pauper or the Grateful Rich Person is Superior
I asked him (may Allah be pleased with him) who was superior between the patient pauper and the grateful rich person. He responded (may Allah be pleased with him) as follows:
The matter of the superiority of the patient pauper over the patient rich person, or the opposite, is well known among the scholars. However, in my opinion, this disagreement is only relevant among the veiled folk who have firm foothold in the realm of realities. According to the people firmly entrenched in the realm of realities, both gratitude and patience is required of them both. 
The reason is that the soul is inclined towards its desires and the fulfillment of its instinctual and human nature. In poverty, that means its fleeing from it and being preoccupied with the requirements for taking flight from poverty. This is due to its seeking to delight in its desires and flee from the punishment and pain of poverty. This situation causes the soul to be distracted from fulfilling the Divine rights and distant from connecting to the Holy Presence. Likewise, in prosperity, it seeks to settle in rest and safety, and to enjoy the sweetness of its desires, seeking permanence in the earth of natural dispositions and instincts. This situation also distracts it from fulfilling the Divine Rights and distances it from connecting with the Holy Presence.
These are the two tests contained in the two afflictions that Allah (Blessed and Exalted is He) mentioned in His words:
{We will afflict them with evil and good as a test. And to us they will be returned. } [al-Anbiya’, 35].
[They will be returned to us] in both situations because the soul’s connection with the Holy Presence causes it to die from its desires, motives and inclinations. That causes it to exit out from its instinct and natural disposition. Thus, there is no share for the soul in that domain. There is only the manifestation of existence by the Real, for the Real, in the Real and from the real. That, along with the distinction of its degrees, differentiating its collectivity and divisibility, recognizing its special qualities and giving everything its due right. That is the essence of complete fulfillment of the Divine Rights. For, in that Presence, it completely fulfills the rights of every one of the Divine Manifestations, the right of every one of the Divine Names and Attributes. And in all that, he is attributed with fulfillment of that which the requirements of the moment necessitate in that Presence. 
If you have understood this, then the rich person who is completely thankful by perfect fulfillment of the Divine rights and firmly established in patience through preventing the soul from remaining in the earth of its natural disposition and instinct, despite its intense inclination towards that and complete weakness. And by enduring the extreme fatigue caused by opposing its natural disposition, he becomes a patient and grateful person. That is because, in that case, his being wealthy is not from the portion of his soul. It is through his firmness in the situation in which Allah has erected him. Thus, it should be clear to you that he is a patient and grateful person because he witnesses himself as His representative in the wealth that He has granted him. It is similar to the situation of the agent with the owner of the wealth. If the owner of the wealth tells him to, he gives. If he tells him to withhold, he withholds. This is evidenced by His words (Exalted is He):
{And spend out of that in which He has made you successors} [al-Hadid, 7].
As for the pauper, if he inculcates, in his soul, connection to the Divine Presence, and it sees the essence of Holy Beauty, he will also be, in his poverty, a patient and grateful person. His gratitude is his perfect fulfillment of the rights of all the Divine Manifestations, collectively and individually, as well as the rights of the Divine Attributes and Names that are revealed to him. So, in all of that, he gives everything its due right. He is not overcome by negligence. Nor, is shocked by the difficulties of calamities because he has become, in everything, standing for Allah, with Allah, from Allah and on behalf of Allah. He pays no attention to anything other than Allah. And he is not satisfied with anything other than Allah. Congruent to his perfection of [his fulfillment] of these rights, he becomes more perfect in his gratitude to his Lord. 
As for his patience, it is his preventing his soul from inclining towards the dictates of its instinct and natural disposition and from its descent into the lowest of levels by inclining towards inaction, the sweetness of its desires and becoming engrossed in the dictates of its ulterior motives by intense flight and distance from what opposes those motives, in terms of the punishment, pain and anguish that accompany poverty. In that case, he is likewise a patient and grateful person because he did not place himself in poverty. Rather, he is firm in the situation in which Allah has erected him. 
Thus, it should be clear to you that they are both equal in that domain. The only caveat to this equality is that the wealthy person may have some defects because of his being free from the exertion that the pauper finds in trying to spend on his family, children, companions, etc. However, this defect is something that is a constant of human nature and does not affect his spirit. And the pauper also has a defect in his finding pain, anguish, difficulty and unpleasantness, at the level of his humanity alone, due to his seeking out that which he is unable to fulfill of his spending on his family, children, companions and others. In proportion to the level of these defects in each of them, there will be differences and superiority of one over the other in their patience and gratitude. 
And if the pauper is transferred to the station of enjoyment of poverty and delighting in its bliss, he will no longer be considered patient. At that moment, he will be grateful in every state. And he will be equal to the grateful wealthy person. But this is only obtained through pure Divine giving. There is no way to obtain it through effort.

This ends what he (may Allah be pleased with him) dictated to us.

Sheikh / Disciple Relationship::
Sheikh / Disciple Relationship: 

meaning with certainty, and give it to al-Tijānī. Tell him . . .” What follows is a lengthy explanation, interspersed with the sort of exhortations a master would give his disciple: “Tell him to exert effort in worship and contraven- ing his carnal self (nafs).” Or, “Tell him that the people of divine manifes- tation (ahl al-tajallā) are those who inherit my spiritual station (maqām).”151
This intriguing account suggests that disciples participated alongside the shaykh in visionary experience. Such participation meant that disciples sometimes assisted the shaykh in the realization of knowledge, or least served as the means by which al-Tijānī learned from the Prophet. It seems that al-Tijānī’s space for spiritual retreat in Abī Samghūn was divided in two, one room for al-Tijānī and another for al-Damrāwī.152 On one occa- sion, the Prophet told al-Tijānī to visit al-Damrāwī and treat him kindly, as “he has a right upon you.”153 But the commendation was mutual. Once al-Damrāwī expressed his love for al-Tijānī to the Prophet. The Prophet revealed to him, “If not for this love of yours for al-Tijānī, you never would have seen me.”154

The remarkably pervasive presence of the Prophet in the life of al-Tijānī and his disciples is difficult to miss. Here the Prophet sometimes took on the role of initiator of the shaykh’s own disciples; and in some cases, used them to initiate the shaykh. In the Mashāhid, ʿAlī Ḥarāzim attests that he found “an old paper” on which al-Tijānī had written, as if to remind himself: “My path is the Ṭarīqa Muḥammadiyya, given to me by the Prophet, from him to me. And my disciples are his disciples.”181

Shaikh al-Tijani (ra)::
Shaikh al-Tijani (ra): 

Know that all enunciated letters (al-ḥurūf al-lafẓiyya) have their semblances in the world of spirits (ʿālam al-arwāḥ). The meaning here is that, with the enunciation of every word, an angel is created who glorifies God the exalted. If you speak a word of good, by this an angel of mercy is created. If you speak a word of evil, by this an angel of punishment is created. If it is God’s decree and the speaker repents from the (evil) statement, the angel (of punishment) created from it is held back and turned into an angel of mercy.” 

—Z Wright 

“Let he who believes in Allah and the Last Day to say that which is good or remain silent.” —Hadith

Shaikh Al-Tijani (ra) quotes thus Aḥmad b. Ḥanbal (d. 855, Baghdad) to say, “Idols (tāghūt) are anything that occupies a person with other than God, even if for one moment.”True tawḥīd was thus the essence of Islam: “The secure end,” al-Tijānī responded when asked about salvation, “is that we are Muslims. But by God, many of us have not smelled the fragrance of Islam.” Z Wright
